@STX
The game was approached like a simulation. The first step was to explore the effects of the different parameters on the general outcome of the game. Once I was able to gain an idea of what was effective and what was not, the next step was to try to optimize the results using incremental changes in the main levers. For example, moving the gravity well had a significant impact on the outcome but required trial and error before the best location was achieved. So in summary, the first step was to try to look at the overall system results from a macro perspective, followed by the second step of refining the details to get as close as possible to the desired results.
